Human Backlog Items:

## Prioritization principle тАФ UI styling Pareto (added 2026-05-16)

UI styling work obeys Pareto: ~20% of the styling effort gets the UI to ~80% тАФ past the interpretability threshold where users can read and use the surface. The remaining 80% of polish effort (micro-spacing, motion, edge-case visual states, theming nuance) compounds slowly and should not block product progress.

**Rule:** when triaging UX-*, A11Y-*, PP-*, or impeccable-extracted polish rows, ask "does shipping this move the surface *from broken/illegible to readable*, or *from readable to refined*?"

- **From broken to readable** тЖТ keep at current priority. Interpretability fixes block usability.
- **From readable to refined** тЖТ demote. Move to ┬з6 (Deferred UI polish) or stack at the bottom of ┬з1. Revisit only after core feature work clears.

Apply during `/next-best-backlog-items` scoring and during `/backlog-sync` re-tiering. This is the user's explicit directive тАФ don't override it without checking in.

## Legend

| Tag | Meaning |
|---|---|
| ЁЯЯв | **Ready** тАФ scoped, unblocked, not yet picked up |
| тЪб | **In progress** тАФ an agent or human is actively working on it |
| ЁЯФО | **In review** тАФ PR open, awaiting review or CI |
| ЁЯзК | **Deferred** тАФ intentionally parked |
| тЬЕ | **Shipped** тАФ moved to ┬з7 |
| ЁЯФ┤ | **Blocked** тАФ prerequisite open; note `Blocked by:` inline |
| ЁЯзС | **Needs human** тАФ account signup, env var, click-through тАФ see ┬з8 |

Every active row **must** include a `Status:` field (`Ready` / `In progress` / `In review` / `Blocked` / `Shipped`) and, when applicable, `Owner:` (agent name or human) and `Branch:`/`PR:` once work starts. `/backlog-sync` fills what it can infer.

**Story-ID prefixes**
- `ON-*` тАФ general stories (mobile a11y, mechanical sweeps, large features)
- `PP-*` тАФ platform parity (web/iOS/Android)
- `A11Y-*` тАФ accessibility tooling
- `UX-*` тАФ deferred UI redesign polish
- `TD-*` тАФ tech debt (newly opened; historical items live in `docs/project-info/technology/TECH_DEBT.md`)
- `OOP-*` тАФ invariant-preserving refactor candidates (see `docs/plans/2026-05-14-oop-refactor.md` and the `/oop` skill)
- `LAUNCH-*` тАФ launch readiness (App Store, EAS, web go-live, observability, compliance)
- `P2-*`..`P5-*` тАФ phase backlogs (all shipped, retained as a log in ┬з7)
- `B*`/`D*`/`A*`/`C*` тАФ before-launch Claude tasks (shipped where no ЁЯзС gate)

| ON-77 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P1 / High** | тАФ | тАФ | **Task data model + RLS + configurable role-based permissions** | Foundational row for the Phase 7 Task-coordination epic (ROADMAP ┬зPhase 7); **blocks ON-79/80/81/82/83/84**. Surfaced 2026-05-20 from a caregiver flow: a coordinator (or the recipient) raises a discrete activity that must be completed, optionally pinned to a shift, with role-gated completion and lifecycle tracking. **Schema:** new `tasks` table тАФ `id, org_id, recipient_id, title, instructions text (markdown), checklist jsonb (ordered clickable to-do items: [{label, done}]), status task_status, assigned_to uuid REFERENCES auth.users, created_by, requested_by uuid (the human who raised it), requested_on_behalf_of uuid NULL REFERENCES care_recipients (set when the recipient is the originator тАФ see ON-83), shift_id uuid NULL REFERENCES shifts(id) ON DELETE SET NULL (pin to current OR future shift), due_at timestamptz NULL, completed_at, completed_by`. New `task_status` enum (`todo`, `in_progress`, `done`, `cancelled`) тАФ string-literal-union on the TS side per code style. **Role-based access (configurable per org by admin):** a capability map deciding (a) which roles may CREATE tasks and (b) which roles may COMPLETE a given task. **Open design decision (resolve in plan):** store as a per-org `task_permissions` config (jsonb on organizations or a dedicated table) keyed by roleтЖТcapability, vs. a per-task `allowed_completer_roles` column, vs. both. Default posture: coordinators always create+complete; admin can widen creation to other roles. RLS via existing `user_can_access_recipient()` / `user_is_org_coordinator()` helpers + a new completion-permission predicate; **pgTAP coverage required** (cross-org rejection, role-gated completion allow/deny, recipient-scope). **Risk:** MEDIUM (new RLS surface тАФ get the completion predicate right). **Size:** L (~1тАУ2 days: migration + enum + RLS + pgTAP + types regen). |
| ON-78 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P2 / Medium** | тАФ | тАФ | **On-call shift type (`shift_type` enum on `shifts`)** | Part of the Phase 7 Task epic (ROADMAP ┬зPhase 7). Adds a shift *type* dimension orthogonal to the existing `shift_status` lifecycle (open/claimed/confirmed/completed/missed). **Schema:** new `shift_type` enum (`standard`, `on_call`); add `shift_type shift_type NOT NULL DEFAULT 'standard'` column to `shifts`; backfill existing rows to `standard` (the DEFAULT covers this). An on-call shift designates its `assigned_to` caregiver as the routing target for task requests arriving during `[starts_at, ends_at)` тАФ consumed by ON-81 (notifications). **Web + mobile shift-create UI** gains a type selector (can fold into this row or split a thin UI follow-up). RLS unchanged (inherits `shifts` policies); add a pgTAP assertion that the new column doesn't widen access. Independent of ON-77 тАФ touches `shifts`, not `tasks`. **Risk:** LOW (additive enum + column + DEFAULT backfill). **Size:** M (~half day: migration + enum + type selector UI + types regen). |

| TD-156 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P3 / Low** | тАФ | тАФ | **Supabase Auth email subjects differ for new vs existing users (minor inbox enumeration)** | Surfaced 2026-05-17 by Cowork auth-unhappy suite run `1778990299` scenario 4. UI is correctly indistinguishable for new vs existing emails ("Check your emailтАж"), but Supabase Auth dispatches different *email templates* server-side: new users get `"Confirm Your Signup"`, existing users get `"Your Magic Link"`. Confirmed via Resend logs (email IDs `43891be0-тАж` for new, `f5498db3-тАж` / `f439c728-тАж` for existing). Practical exploit value: essentially nil тАФ an attacker with mailbox access already has full compromise. But it's worth standardizing the templates for clean threat model. **Fix:** in Supabase Dashboard тЖТ Auth тЖТ Email Templates, set "Confirm Signup" and "Magic Link" templates to identical subject lines (e.g. both `"Your CareSync sign-in code"`). **Risk:** LOW. **Size:** XS (~10 min in Supabase dashboard). |
| TD-157 | ЁЯЯб Spike ┬╖ **P2 / Medium** | тАФ | тАФ | **Spike: does requesting a fresh OTP revoke existing sessions for same user?** | Surfaced 2026-05-17 by Cowork auth-unhappy suite run `1778990299` scenario 5 (inconclusive). Empirical signal: Tab A signed in successfully (session cookie present, `/dashboard` rendered); after Tab B fired a fresh OTP request for the same email, Tab A's URL was back at `/signin`. If reproducible, requesting a new OTP for an existing user revokes their existing sessions тАФ atypical for Supabase Auth and potentially user-hostile (a malicious actor knowing an email could log a user out by triggering OTP requests). Tab navigation noise during the test makes attribution unreliable. **Repro steps:** sign in with email X in tab A; from tab B, fire OTP request for email X; immediately check tab A's session via `/dashboard` reload (no human-driven tab switches). Document actual behavior. If it reproduces, file as a bug-fix follow-up. **Risk:** LOW (read-only investigation). **Size:** XS (~20 min). |

| ID | Status | Story | Notes |

### Onboarding bugs (ON-75)

| ID | Status | Story | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| ON-75 | ЁЯЯб Pending verification (local) | **Onboarding wizard тАФ care team setup failure was misconfigured local env, not an RLS policy gap** | Root cause amended 2026-05-10 PM. Initial repro showed `Error: Org creation failed: new row violates row-level security policy for table "organizations"`. Diagnosis traced it to `apps/web/.env.local` containing the **production** `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` in `sb_secret_*` format, which the local Supabase JWT-only auth rejected тАФ `supabaseAdmin` silently fell back to anon role, then RLS correctly blocked the insert. The route + repository code are correct; the server-side `supabaseAdmin` client bypasses RLS when the key is valid. Resolution: swap local `.env.local` to the JWT from `supabase status` (owner action, hook-protected). **Verify in production** тАФ if production deploy actually has a valid service role key (likely yes), prod is unaffected and this row closes as "config issue". If prod also fails, reopen as a real RLS gap. Defense-in-depth follow-up: surface a clearer error than a generic RLS message when `supabaseAdmin` is misconfigured (file as TD if it recurs). |

### OWASP audit follow-ups (SEC-002..006, TD-131..132) тАФ opened 2026-05-14

Source: `/owasp` full-project read-only audit. Findings at `docs/security/2026-05-14-owasp-audit.md`. 1 High + 3 Medium + 2 Low (1 Info dropped тАФ no action). All file:line cited and grep-verified. Mostly defense-in-depth gaps on an otherwise strong posture (34/34 tables RLS-enabled, no XSS/code-exec sinks, PHI invariant double-enforced).

| ID | Status | Story | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| SEC-007 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #531 | OCR confirm route audit-log site (FIND-003 part 3) | Append-only `ocr_audit_log` table тАФ PHI-free by construction (SHA-256 of `raw_text` NFC-normalized + `confirmed_field_keys` allowlist text[], never values). Defense-in-depth append-only via BOTH triggers AND `REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE` (covers `session_replication_role='replica'` bypass per cycle-1 Opus review). Service-role-only RLS policy. Audit insert lands BEFORE medication insert; failure returns 500 (fail-loud). Per-attempt semantics тАФ records 409-losers too. 10 pgTAP cases (RLS, append-only, CHECK constraints, FK RESTRICT). Backfill placeholder rows for existing `status='confirmed'` jobs with empty-string hash marker + `backfilled=true`. /opus-on-opus cleared cycle 2 (0/0/1). Follow-ups seeded: TD-144 (atomic confirm RPC), TD-145 (DDL lint CONCURRENTLY annotation). |

Story can sit blocked until an AI feature adds an INSERT. **Risk:** LOW. **Size:** S (1тАУ2h). |
| SEC-008 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P3 / Low** | **Rotate existing 128/192-bit share tokens to 256-bit** | SEC-006 #492 changed `outer_circle_requests.share_token` and `care_briefs.share_token` DEFAULTs to 256-bit but did NOT rotate existing in-flight tokens. Existing tokens still exceed the 64-bit guessability floor (128-bit minimum is OWASP-compliant) so this is consistency cleanup, not vuln remediation. Implementation: new migration that regenerates each existing `share_token` with `gen_random_bytes(32)`, PLUS a notification email to outer-circle requesters / care-brief owners that their old link is invalidated. **Risk:** MEDIUM (link invalidation is user-visible тАФ requires the email step). **Size:** M (2тАУ3h). |

| TD-137 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #520 | JournalCard author lookup: useMemo'd Map<user_id, display_name> hoisted to JournalTimeline | Pure refactor; O(N├ЧM) per-render .find() тЖТ O(M) memo + O(1) gets. Path (a) chosen; path (b) (pre-resolve into useJournalData state) deferred. |

| TD-139 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #513 | PDF export: payload.note/notes fallback when text empty | Shipped via `pickJournalBody` helper in `apps/web/lib/`; 7-case unit test locks precedence text > note > notes. |
| TD-140 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #514 | memberships test: filter-contract assertions on getCareTeamForRecipient | Test-only; locks select/eq/or shape on prod query. .not() deferred. |
| TD-141 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P3 / Low** | **JournalPayload: consolidate `text`/`note`/`notes` parallel free-text slots into one `body` field** | Surfaced 2026-05-15 by `/oop --from-sprint` review of TD-139 (PR #513). `JournalPayload` at `apps/web/lib/careEvent.ts:49-54` has three parallel optional string fields. In-repo there are now 3 different policies for picking the "primary body": `handoffSummary.ts:148` reads `text` only; `VisitSummary.tsx:395-397` uses `note ?? notes`; `pickJournalBody.ts` uses `text > note > notes`. Long-term: schema migration to a single `body` column on `journal_events`, then call-site sweep + delete the three slots. **Risk:** MEDIUM (migration touches `journal_events` table, needs backfill of `text`тЖТ`body` then `note`/`notes`тЖТ`body` with precedence). **Size:** M (~half-day; needs separate plan + ADR for the precedence choice). |
| TD-142 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ 2026-05-17 ┬╖ PR #567 | **Collapse parallel invite-acceptance state machines (TS `acceptInvite` vs SQL `accept_invite`)** | Surfaced 2026-05-15 by `/oop --from-sprint` review of the careteam-rls-defense sprint. Both `acceptInvite` (`apps/web/server/repositories/membershipsRepository.ts:163-200`) and the `accept_invite(text, uuid, text)` SQL function (introduced in migration `20260407_atomic_invite_accept.sql`, locked-down by `20260516000000_revoke_accept_invite_from_anon_authenticated.sql`) encode the same state transition: validate token тЖТ check expiry тЖТ check consumed тЖТ check email match тЖТ mark consumed + activate membership. The TS version has a known atomicity hole тАФ `Promise.all` of two updates is **not** a real DB transaction (called out in its own comment at `:182-185`: "A Postgres RPC function would be the correct fix"). The SQL version is exactly that, currently dead code defended only by the REVOKE migration. **Decision needed:** (a) flip `acceptInvite` to `supabaseAdmin.rpc('accept_invite', ...)` and delete the TS body тАФ gains atomicity; OR (b) drop the SQL function + migration + pgTAP cases 7тАУ9 entirely тАФ loses a defense layer. Every future invite-rule change (single-use enforcement, audit log, rate limit) currently has to land in two places that disagree on atomicity guarantees. **Risk:** MEDIUM (path-dependent). **Size:** SтАУM. |
| TD-144 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ 2026-05-17 ┬╖ PR #589 | тАФ | тАФ | **Atomic OCR confirm via SECURITY DEFINER RPC** | Resolution: new `confirm_ocr_job(...)` SECURITY DEFINER function takes `FOR UPDATE` on `ocr_jobs` row and collapses audit insert + medication insert + status flip into one transaction. Sentinel return struct (`success, error`) replaces optimistic-lock count check. Route handler rewrites to thin RPC caller with sentinelтЖТHTTP map. 18 pgTAP assertions cover function metadata + privilege grants + happy path + race-loser contract + 4 sentinel paths + empty-array COALESCE. Also fixed latent bug: prior route passed `created_by` to `medications` but column doesn't exist (PostgREST silently dropped). /oop surfaced TD-174/175/176 (race-test annotation, scan_source backfill, Sentry tag convention). |
| TD-145 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #533 | migration-lint: whitelist CREATE INDEX on same-file new tables | `scripts/migration-lint.sh` now pre-scans normalized statements for CREATE TABLE [IF NOT EXISTS] <name>, then skips the CONCURRENTLY check for CREATE INDEX whose ON-target is in that set. Handles schema-qualified + quoted identifiers via shared regex normalization (lowercased, schema prefix stripped, quotes stripped) compared via `grep -Fxq`. Bash discipline: `|| true` after grep -E to survive `set -e`; POSIX ERE only (no -P, no \b). 9-case dev-gate test harness at `scripts/__tests__/migration-lint.test.sh` (NOT wired into CI; CI keeps invoking the production script via `.github/workflows/migration-lint.yml:28`). Closes the SEC-007 post-merge advisory + prevents future "new table + index in one migration" false positives. /opus-on-opus cleared cycle 2 (2MF/3SF/2N тЖТ 0/1/2). |
| TD-146 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ 2026-05-17 ┬╖ PR #559 | **Audit prod Inngest cron-firing state тАФ verify the 14 functions actually run** | **Partial finding (2026-05-16, during SEC-001 rotation):** hypothesis #2 confirmed тАФ crons DO fire and show under **Functions тЖТ Runs** (weekly-digest had 3 runs in last 24h); the "0 events in 24h" reading on the Events tab was metric semantics (Events tab tracks `inngest.send()` calls, not cron triggers). Inngest app reachable post-rotation (Last seen ticks; manual Invoke succeeds). **Remaining work:** still need per-function firing audit for all 14 functions to confirm none are env-gated dark тАФ especially `rateLimit429Monitor` (every 5 min) and `shiftTradeExpiry` (every 15 min) which dominate the projected ~387 firings/day. Original three hypotheses for posterity: (1) **Prod Inngest app not registered or unreachable** тАФ verify via Inngest dashboard тЖТ Apps тЖТ carelog тЖТ "Last seen" timestamp; if stale, the SDK isn't reaching Inngest cloud. Fix: confirm `INNGEST_SIGNING_KEY` + `INNGEST_EVENT_KEY` are set on prod Vercel env (these were also part of SEC-001 rotation scope) AND that the `/api/inngest` endpoint is publicly reachable from Inngest cloud. (2) **Dashboard 1-day window is reading a narrower metric than total runs** тАФ eyeball whether "Functions" tab shows per-function run counts differently from the top-line "Events". (3) **High-frequency crons silently disabled** тАФ `rateLimit429Monitor` (every 5 min) and `shiftTradeExpiry` (every 15 min) dominate the projected count; check `apps/web/inngest/functions/` for any env-gated short-circuits. **Deliverable:** capture the actual prod cron firing pattern (which functions, how often, last successful run) in a follow-up note appended to the research doc ┬з6.6, OR open targeted bug-fix rows if any cron is dark. **Blocks:** any decision on Inngest-vs-Queues migration (TD-133, ON-70, ON-71) тАФ the cost half of the ┬з6 recommendation is structurally unverifiable until prod firing state is known. **Risk:** LOW (read-only investigation). **Size:** S (~30 min). |

Three to five long-form articles on caregiver pain points: "Managing medications across a care team", "Sharing shift handoff notes that actually help", "When a parent's care needs grow beyond what one person can do", etc. Each article is internally linked, has its own JSON-LD `Article` markup, and lands in the sitemap. ~8 hr тАФ **6 of those 8 are long-form copy writing where single creative voice matters; flagged ЁЯзС Needs human.** Infra (~2 hr) can be ready when the human carves out the writing time. |
| SEO-007 | ЁЯзС Needs human | **Verify in Google Search Console + Bing Webmaster Tools, submit sitemap** | Both consoles require ownership verification (DNS TXT or meta tag тАФ meta tag works since marketing routes are SSG). Ownership tag goes in `(marketing)/layout.tsx`. Then submit `https://care-log.org/sitemap.xml`. Track index coverage weekly for the first month. Mostly setup, but gates SEO-001..006's measurable impact. ~30 min once human is at the keyboard. |

### Lighthouse a11y CI gating gap (TD-87) тАФ opened 2026-04-29

Discovered during `/impeccable critique` post-merge verification of PR #269. The CI Lighthouse a11y workflow ran on the merged main but reported "success" without auditing anything тАФ Vercel preview deployments are auth-gated (HTTP 401), and `scripts/lighthouse-a11y.mjs:27-33` treats 401/403 as a non-blocking skip. Net effect: the a11y score gate has been silently inactive on every preview-driven CI run. Local Lighthouse on the actual marketing routes still passed (96 / 100 / 94 on /, /about, /pricing) so no regression slipped through this time, but the gate is not protecting us.

| ID | Status | Story | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| TD-87 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ 2026-05-18 ┬╖ PRs #602 / #603 | **Restore Lighthouse a11y gating in CI тАФ path b chosen** | Resolution: 2-PR ship. Path-pick decision (b) recorded in ADR-0005. PR #602 swapped trigger from `deployment_status` тЖТ `pull_request` with broad `paths:` filter, build + `pnpm start` + `npx wait-on` (mirrors ci.yml E2E block), audit `/`, `/pricing`, `/about` via `node scripts/lighthouse-a11y.mjs`. Script: N-URL aggregation, removed 401/403 silent-skip, pinned `@lhci/cli@0.15.1`. PR #602 first run surfaced a pre-existing script bug (`@lhci/cli collect --outputPath` is a no-op; lhci writes to `.lighthouseci/lhr-*.json` in cwd) тАФ masked for months by the silent-skip path. PR #603 hot-fix: per-URL tempdir + readdir `.lighthouseci/` + `--numberOfRuns=1`. Verified end-to-end: `/`=100, `/pricing`=96, `/about`=96. NOT a required check in v1 per ADR-0005; promotion needs `merge_group` trigger first. /oop residual: TD-184. |
| TD-170b | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ 2026-05-18 ┬╖ PR #605 (investigation) | тАФ | тАФ | **Root-cause E2E chronic-red on main** | Resolution: investigation report at `docs/notes/2026-05-18-td-170b-e2e-investigation.md` тАФ root cause was UX-04x copy-audit trio (PRs #525/#528/#529, all 2026-05-15) renaming UI strings without sweeping E2E. Retro-validation re-confirmed against PRs #525/#528/#529. |

### Hardening audit (TD-94..104, A11Y-019, UX-053) тАФ opened 2026-04-29

Source: `/impeccable harden` audit against the whole web app on 2026-04-29 (`/tmp/harden-audit-2026-04-29.md`). 184 source files / 13 `(app)` routes scanned. Findings ranked High/Med/Low. The four High-severity items (TD-94, TD-96, TD-97, TD-99) are file-disjoint and TDD-friendly тАФ natural fit for a 4-track `/dispatch` wave. Items already in good shape (reduced motion, mood color+text pairing, focus rings, logical CSS direction, offline queue architecture) intentionally **not** filed.

| ID | Status | Story | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| TD-94 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #304 | **`AbortController` for in-effect fetches + tRPC** | High severity. Zero `AbortController` usages across the entire web app. Every `useEffect`-triggered `fetch` and every tRPC query that fires during navigation continues to completion after unmount; race conditions on fast tab-switching (e.g. between recipients on `/journal/[recipientId]`) can stomp later state with earlier responses. Confirmed site: `apps/web/app/(app)/journal/[recipientId]/JournalTimeline.tsx` raw `fetch(url)` in effect with no signal. Fix: add a `useAbortable` hook in `apps/web/hooks/`, plumb `signal` through all in-effect fetches and tRPC queries that own a long-lived subscription. ~3 hr. |
| TD-95 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #305 | **Explicit `Intl.*Format` instances in `lib/format.ts`** | High severity. TD-88 just shipped 11 date/time helpers but they still rely on the runtime locale with `.toLocaleDateString` / `.toLocaleTimeString` and no explicit options. Net `Intl.*Format` usage in app code (excl. comments) = zero. Locale-stable formatting is impossible to test, dates render inconsistently SSR vs. client, and there's no path to localized number/currency. Migrate the helpers to construct cached `Intl.DateTimeFormat` / `Intl.NumberFormat` / `Intl.RelativeTimeFormat` instances with explicit options. Pairs with TD-104. ~2 hr. |
| TD-96 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #306 | **Surface every mutation failure in journal panels** | High severity. 6 silent / lossy `catch {}` blocks in journal flows. `JournalTimeline.tsx:106` swallows network errors after an optimistic update with only "Rollback on network error" тАФ no toast, no surface. `OuterCirclePanel.tsx:97` is fully silent. `OcrReviewPanel.tsx:85`, `ExportButton.tsx:61`, `OuterCirclePanel.tsx:87` set local error state but never surface it via toast. User gets no signal that their action failed (especially bad when the optimistic update made it look like the action succeeded). Standardize: every `catch` in a mutation path emits a sonner toast with retry affordance + rolls back optimistic state. ~3 hr. |
| TD-97 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #307 | **`disabled={mutation.isPending}` on every form submit** | High severity. ~11 disabled-while-pending guards across all submit handlers. Most submit buttons are not disabled while the mutation is in flight тАФ mashing Submit on a slow connection enqueues N duplicate inserts. Highest risk on the offline-queue path, which already replays writes. Audit every `<form onSubmit>` and every primary action button calling a `useMutation`; add `disabled={mutation.isPending}` + idempotency assertion where the server can't dedupe. Test plan: a single component test per form that simulates 5 rapid clicks and asserts the mutation fired exactly once. ~4 hr. |
| TD-98 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #334 | **Text overflow / truncation pass on cards** | Med severity. `apps/web/components/dashboard/MedCard.tsx:192-200`: `<span className="flex-1 тАж">{med.name} ┬╖ {med.dose}</span>` has no `min-w-0` / `truncate`. A 60-char drug name (e.g. *"Methylphenidate hydrochloride extended-release 36 mg"*) overflows the card or pushes the Log button off-screen on 320px. The `aria-label` on the Log button also inflates. Same risk: RecipientHeader, ShiftEventCard, JournalTimeline entry titles. Apply `min-w-0 truncate` (or 2-line clamp) and add a 60+ char fixture to the relevant component test. ~2 hr. |
| TD-99 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #302 | **Per-route `error.tsx` boundaries** | High severity. Only `/dashboard` and `/journal/[recipientId]` have `error.tsx` boundaries. Settings, Messages, Education, Subscriptions, Billing, Visit Summary, History Export, Team Admin all crash to the root error boundary on any render error тАФ losing in-flight form state. Add per-route `error.tsx` with retry + "go back" affordance to all 8 missing routes. ~2 hr. |
| TD-100 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #336 | **Journal timeline cursor pagination + virtualization** | Med severity. `JournalTimeline.tsx` renders all DOM nodes for the recipient тАФ a recipient with 2000 journal entries (a year of daily logs + meds) creates a heavy DOM tree. No `react-window` / `@tanstack/virtual` / cursor on the read path. Add cursor pagination + `IntersectionObserver` "load more" with a 200-entry threshold for client-side render. ~4 hr. |
| TD-101 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #333 | **RTL smoke test** | Med severity. 107 tailwind logical-direction utility usages (`ms-/me-/ps-/pe-`) тАФ solid baseline. But: zero `dir="rtl"` test fixture, custom CSS in `globals.css` uses physical properties in spots, app-shell rail is left-anchored without an inline-start variant. Not currently a shipped concern, but if CareSync expands to Spanish-speaking caregivers (a real persona) the editorial Fraunces blocks need an RTL audit. Add an RTL smoke test that loads `/dashboard` with `dir="rtl"` and screenshots the result. ~2 hr. |
| TD-102 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #329 | **`mutations.retry: 0` in TrpcProvider** | Med severity. `apps/web/components/providers/TrpcProvider.tsx:16` sets `retry: 1` globally. For idempotent reads this is fine; for the implicit retries on `useMutation` it's silent and may double-write if the request reached the server but the response was lost. Set `mutations.retry: 0` explicitly; add explicit retry buttons on the surfaces that need them (handled by TD-96). ~0.5 hr. |
| TD-103 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #331 | **Debounce journal + messages search inputs** | Low severity. No debounce on the journal search/filter inputs (sampled `JournalTimeline` filter row). `useMemo` filtering 200+ entries per keystroke is OK locally but stutters on cheap Android. Wrap journal filter in 200ms debounce; same pass for `/messages` search. Pairs naturally with TD-100. ~1 hr. |
| TD-104 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #330 | **`pluralize(count, singular, plural)` helper** | Low severity. Currently zero `count !== 1 ? 's' : ''` ternaries (good тАФ already cleaner than typical) but no helper exists either, so the pattern will reappear. Add `pluralize()` helper using `Intl.PluralRules` (or a thin string fallback); migrate 5тАУ10 sites where "1 entry" / "2 entries" is currently hardcoded. Pairs with TD-95. ~1 hr. |
| A11Y-019 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #332 | **SR-only live region for offline-queue + optimistic-update transitions** | Med severity. 23 `aria-live` / `role=status` usages across the app тАФ sounds like coverage but most are decorative. The optimistic-update path in `JournalTimeline.tsx` and the offline-queue replay flow have **no live region** to announce "logged" / "queued offline" / "synced" / "rollback" to a screen reader. Mood color+text pairing rule is already honored everywhere sampled. Add a single SR-only `aria-live="polite"` region that subscribes to offline-queue events and optimistic-update rollbacks. ~1.5 hr. |
| A11Y-020 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #438 | **`/signin` "Continue with email" button text fails WCAG AA contrast** | Discovered 2026-05-10 smoke walk. The primary CTA on `/signin` renders white text on `--color-primary-light` (`#E48A4A`) тЖТ ~2.5:1 contrast, well below the 4.5:1 AA floor for body text. Other primary CTAs across the app use `--color-primary` (`#D2691E`, ~3.45:1 тАФ still borderline) or `--color-primary-pressed` (`#9C4A14`, 5.67:1 тЬУ AA). Fix: change the SignInForm submit button background to `--color-primary-pressed` OR use the `--color-primary` deeper variant with darker text. Audit the rest of the app for the same anti-pattern (any button using `--color-primary-light` as its base background with white text). Touches `apps/web/app/signin/SignInForm.tsx` + sweep. |
| A11Y-021 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #446 | **Sweep 30+ white-on-`--color-primary` CTAs across app + marketing for AA contrast** | Surfaced during A11Y-020 implementation 2026-05-10. PR #438 fixed signin only; the sweep grep (`bg-[var(--color-primary)]` paired with white/cream foreground) returned 30+ sites. Categories: marketing CTAs (HeroSection, MarketingNav, PricingCards, ContactForm, ForReferrersPage, HowItWorks), in-app buttons (ShiftsPanel, settings, history-export, dashboard, care-share, HandoffSummary), badges/chips (ThreadList, AppTabBar, TimeRailTimeline, MedCard, MedicationChipBar, TagFilter, SageRail), and AI surfaces (AIPanel, AIChatThread). White-on-`#D2691E` тЙИ 3.80:1 тАФ fails 4.5:1 AA for body text but may pass large-text 3:1 floor for badges. Per-site decision: migrate body-text-sized CTAs to `--color-primary-pressed` (`#9C4A14`, ~5.04:1 тЬУ); keep large-text badges where they pass 3:1. ~3 hr. |
| UX-053 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #537 | EmptyState primary-action affordances + passive-site documentation | Audit of 6 EmptyState consumers; none used the component's actionLabel/onAction props. Hoisted CTAs into MedicationPanel ("Add medication", coordinator-gated тЖТ setShowForm) and TeamPanel ("Invite a member", canInvite + !showInvite gated тЖТ onToggleInvite тАФ `!showInvite` guard prevents desktop dead-click on always-visible Invite form, opus cycle-1 catch). 4 intentionally-passive sites (DocumentVault, JournalTimeline, MedicationLinkedDocs, MedicationRecentEvents) annotated with `// UX-053: passive тАФ <reason>` comments so future audits skip. /opus-on-opus cleared cycle 1 (0/2/1). Existing TeamPanel + MedicationPanel + EmptyState tests stay green (33/33). |

### Test gap stories (TD-24..28) тАФ opened 2026-04-25 from coverage analysis

Snapshot at filing time: web 66.74% / mobile 78.53% / RLS 211 tests across 26 files. These five close the highest-leverage PHI/auth/payment gaps. ~12 hr total. **Target after this batch ships:** web тЙе78%, mobile тЙе85%, RLS adds 2 dedicated PHI-table files.

| ID | Status | Story | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| TD-24 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #146 | **`care_events_rls.test.sql`** | `care_events` is the most-frequently-written PHI table (every journal entry) and has NO dedicated RLS test file today (only `care_event_comments` does). A cross-recipient SELECT/INSERT leak would be silent in CI. Test coordinator/aide/outer-circle SELECT and INSERT isolation тАФ especially the cross-recipient leak vector. ~2 hr. |
| TD-25 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #158 | **`supabaseServer` session-refresh unit test** | New file: `apps/web/lib/__tests__/supabaseServer.test.ts`. Cookie-API regressions from Next.js or `@supabase/ssr` upgrades currently have no regression net (route tests mock the client). Simulate expired `access_token` + valid `refresh_token` in cookies, verify a new session is returned (or 401 thrown cleanly). Silent-break vector for ALL SSR routes. ~3 hr. |
| TD-26 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #159 | **`useOfflineWrite` error/retry branch coverage** | Branch coverage is 50% (lines 79-80, 87, 95-96 тАФ the offline retry and error-clear paths). Exactly the code that runs during intermittent connectivity, the most common mobile failure mode. Test: network failure mid-sync (queue not removed), repeated retry on permanent 4xx, queue clear on success. ~2 hr. |
| TD-27 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #153 | **Aide cross-recipient scoping integration test** | New file: `apps/web/server/routers/__tests__/careEventsRouter.scope.test.ts`. RLS covers DB-layer isolation but the tRPC `where` clause is untested for cross-org isolation. Use a real local DB; assert `careEvents.list` called with a `recipient_id` the aide is NOT a member of returns empty (or 403), not data. ~3 hr. |
| TD-28 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #160 | **`messagingPush` + `educationTipRefresh` Inngest failure tests** | These are the only 2 Inngest functions with zero test coverage (out of 11). `messagingPush` fans out push notifications to potentially all family members тАФ an unhandled `DeviceNotRegistered` error would silently drop the job. Test malformed payload + `DeviceNotRegistered` + Expo API timeout. ~2 hr. |
| TD-30 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #149 | **Path-filtered required CI checks (cut rebase wait time)** | 12 required checks fire on every PR including `Mobile тАФ Android debug build` (~3 min) and `RLS pgTAP tests` (~2.5 min) even when no mobile/SQL code changed. With 5 stacked PRs the rebase cascade burns ~30 min of CI per merge cycle. Fix: in `.github/workflows/ci.yml`, scope expensive jobs with `paths:` filters; introduce a single fast `ci-summary` meta-job that always runs and reports the required check name regardless of which downstream jobs fired. Move the 12 specific check names off `required_status_checks` and replace with one `ci-summary`. Branch protection unchanged in spirit тАФ every PR still has to pass тАФ but a docs-only PR finishes in ~30s instead of ~5min. ~2 hr (workflow YAML + branch-protection PATCH). |
| TD-32 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #154 | **Run E2E (Playwright) on PR pushes** | E2E was previously only running on push-to-main; PRs got no Playwright coverage. Re-enabled via `pull_request:` trigger; now in CI Summary. |
| TD-35 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #187 | **Fix TD-30 path-filter false-skip on lockfile-only PRs** | TD-30's per-job `if:` used `contains(toJSON(github.event.pull_request.changed_files), 'apps/web')` тАФ but `changed_files` is an INTEGER (file count), not a path list, so the predicate was always false and every test job silently SKIPPED on every PR. CI Summary treats SKIPPED as pass, so deps bumps shipped without test verification (e.g. TD-29 #165). Fix: replace with SHA-pinned `dorny/paths-filter@v3` doing real glob-based path matching; new `changes` job exposes `web`/`mobile`/`supabase`/`deps`/`e2e` outputs that downstream jobs gate on via `needs:`. |
| TD-36 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #173 | **Mobile lockfile management тАФ pnpm-monorepo compatibility** | Investigation found apps/mobile already in `pnpm-workspace.yaml` + `pnpm-lock.yaml`; the npm-format `package-lock.json` was a stale orphan from a prior `npm install`. Path (a) chosen: deleted the orphan + added to `.gitignore` + documented `pnpm install` requirement in `apps/mobile/CLAUDE.md`. Mobile tests 33 pass / 15 skip (matches baseline); Expo CLI resolves post-install. |
| TD-41 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #178 | **PostHog uninitialized in CI breaks every form-submit** | CI doesn't set `NEXT_PUBLIC_POSTHOG_KEY`. Server `lib/posthog-server.ts` constructs `new PostHog(undefined!)` which throws "You must pass your PostHog project's api key" тАФ surfaced as 500 from `/api/onboarding/create` and every other event-capturing route. Browser-side, `posthog.capture()` / `posthog.identify()` calls in `SignInForm` + `OnboardingForm` threw the same message, aborting the submit handler **before** `router.replace('/dashboard')`. Form silently stayed on /signin or /onboarding; `waitForURL` timed out тАФ the visible CI symptom. Fix: server returns no-op stub when no key; client inits with placeholder + `opt_out_capturing()` when no key. Bundles a Next 16 hydration fix in `app/layout.tsx` (anti-FOUC `<script>` was a direct child of `<html>`, hard-failing hydration in React 19). |
| TD-42 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #180 | **`ensureCareTeam` helper selector drift тАФ dashboard "View care journal" is a `<p>` not a `<button>`** | `e2e/helpers.ts:91,100,110` waits for `button:has-text("View care journal")`. The dashboard renders that string as `<p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">` inside a clickable `<Card onClick>` (see `apps/web/app/(app)/dashboard/DashboardClient.tsx:319-323`), so the selector never matches and `ensureCareTeam` times out for any test using it. Slipped in with TD-40 (#177). Fix: replace the three selectors with `text="View care journal"` (or scope to the parent Card heading). Once landed, ai-assistant.spec progresses past `beforeEach` and the remaining 4 consent-modal failures become visible (separate diagnosis). |

### CareSync 2.0 design handoff (UX-054..UX-060) тАФ opened 2026-04-30

Source: second design prototype handoff (`docs/design/caresync-2-0/`, plan at `docs/design/caresync-2-0-plan.md`). The 2026-04-23 prior handoff (UX-14..UX-21) shipped BriefHero + Fraunces typography + Patterns strip + Handoff modal тАФ gap-audited 2026-04-30 to drop those and the marketing hero (already editorial). Net new: Sage palette behind a theme switcher (violet stays default), card-header variants, Now Board, Meds schedule + adherence, Shifts Briefing/Lanes/Now-board, Journal prompted composer + mood spectrum + heatmap, recipient profile card. Six tracks; UX-054 is foundation, UX-055 is utility, UX-056..UX-060 fan out in parallel.

| ID | Status | Story | Notes |

Medications confirmed via OCR before this migration deployed have a different `scan_source` than those confirmed after тАФ any analytics/UI/query filter segmenting on `scan_source='ocr_scan'` will silently miss the pre-migration cohort. **Fix:** one-time SQL migration that UPDATEs `medications` where a matching `ocr_jobs` row exists with `status='confirmed'` to set `scan_source='ocr_scan'`. **Risk:** LOW (idempotent UPDATE; no schema change). **Size:** XS (~20 min migration + pgTAP). |

| ЁЯЪй TD-189 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P1 / High тАФ pick first** | тАФ | тАФ | **Backlog hygiene upgrades тАФ row template + sharded backlog + pre-flight row-verification skill** | Surfaced 2026-05-18 during a session-retrospective on /sprint pipeline efficacy. (3) **Pre-flight row-verification skill** (`/verify-row <id>`) тАФ runs before /sprint Step 4 (implementation-plan): re-greps target file paths against current source, diffs row's claims against actual code, surfaces drift to the planner BEFORE the plan is written. Returns "row is current" / "row is stale: <diffs>" / "row is wrong: <evidence>". `/sprint` skill change: between Step 3 (Gate 1) and Step 3b, fire `/verify-row` on each row in the chunk; any non-current row blocks until user acknowledges or row is rewritten. **Risk:** MEDIUM (touches BACKLOG-as-SoT contract; sharding migration is high-blast-radius). **Size:** M (~half-day with planning; possibly 2-track wave: sharding migration + template/skill in parallel). **Plan:** `docs/plans/2026-05-18-td-189-backlog-hygiene-upgrades.md`. | TD-190a | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P2 / Medium** ┬╖ blocked-by TD-189 | тАФ | тАФ | **Multi-session skill: `/dispatch-sprint-session` тАФ spawn worker session with handoff** | Surfaced 2026-05-18 during retrospective on parallel-session driver pattern (alternative to in-session subagent dispatch). | TD-190c | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P2 / Medium** ┬╖ blocked-by TD-189 | тАФ | тАФ | **Multi-session skill: `/reserve-chunk` тАФ atomic claim with timeout** | Surfaced 2026-05-18 with TD-190 family. Writes `.claude/state/multi-sprint/reservations.json` with `{td-189: {session: abc123, claimed-at: <ts>}}`. Blocks other `/reserve-chunk` calls on the same id. Document the choice in the skill. **Why blocked by TD-189:** row-IDs as lock keys assume the sharded backlog's stable per-row identity. **Risk:** MEDIUM (correctness-critical for multi-session; bugs cause double-work). **Size:** S (~2h). |
| TD-190d | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P3 / Low** ┬╖ blocked-by TD-189 | тАФ | тАФ | **Multi-session skill: `/serialize-close-out` тАФ driver-owned PR merge serializer** | Surfaced 2026-05-18 with TD-190 family. Driver-owned wrapper that workers ping with "ready to close"; driver picks ONE to merge `BACKLOG.md` changes first, rebases the others, merges in serial order to prevent ┬з0 row-count race. **CAVEAT:** likely collapses to a `/backlog-sync` re-run once TD-189 sharded-backlog lands тАФ sharding makes `BACKLOG.md` updates atomic per-shard rather than adjacent-row, so the row-count race vanishes. Re-evaluate scope after TD-189 ships: this may downgrade to "delete; subsumed by post-sharding /backlog-sync." **Risk:** LOW. **Size:** XS post-TD-189 if needed at all. |
| TD-192 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P3 / Low** | тАФ | тАФ | **Extend TD-178 stable-error-code pattern across the repository layer + normalize update path + Sentry cause hygiene** | Surfaced 2026-05-19 by `/oop --from-sprint` on the TD-178/182/184 sprint (findings S1 + S2). Three coordinated cleanups: **(a)** `apps/web/server/repositories/membershipsRepository.ts:23, 80, 161, 219, 232` тАФ 5 sibling throw sites still use `throw new Error(\`<context> failed: ${error?.message}\`)`. Same PHI defense-in-depth concern as TD-178 (`Memberships fetch failed: тАж`, `getCareTeamForRecipient failed: тАж`, `getRefillRecipients failed: тАж`, `Membership creation failed: тАж`, `Invite token creation failed: тАж`). Migrate each to `throw new Error("<stable_code>", { cause: error })` with matching test updates. **(b)** `apps/web/server/repositories/identityRepository.ts:145` тАФ `updateEmergencyInfo` still throws `identity_update_failed: ${code}` with the code suffixed to `.message`. T1 (TD-178) shipped `identity_read_failed` / `identity_create_failed` as code-only message + `cause:` form. Normalize on the cause-bearing form so all 3 identityRepository throw sites have the same contract. Update test at line 451 to assert `err.cause.code === "23505"` instead of `err.message === "identity_update_failed: 23505"`. **(c)** Sentry serialization hygiene тАФ `Error("тАж", { cause: pgError })` preserves the raw Postgres error object via `.cause`. Default Sentry serialization walks `cause` and can surface column values to log aggregators. Either (i) strip `cause` before `Sentry.captureException`, OR (ii) install a `beforeSend` hook that walks `cause` and redacts message/detail fields. Document the choice in `apps/web/sentry.server.config.ts` + add a sentinel test. **Risk:** LOW. **Size:** S (~1.5h all 3 тАФ 5 throw sites + 1 normalize + 1 Sentry config). |
| TD-193 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P3 / Low** | тАФ | тАФ | **Extract `resolveMembershipsToUsers` shared helper тАФ deduplicate chunked-allSettled rate-limit pattern** | Surfaced 2026-05-19 by `/oop --from-sprint` on the TD-178/182/184 sprint (finding S3). `getCareTeamForRecipient` (lines 84-115) and `getRefillRecipients` (lines 166-194) both own identical `CARE_TEAM_CHUNK_SIZE=8` chunking around `Promise.allSettled` + per-row `supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.getUserById` + `console.warn("тАж: getUserById rejected", reason)` on rejected settlement. Same Auth Admin rate-limit policy (50/s/project); two implementations. **Fix:** extract `resolveMembershipsToUsers<T>(rows, mapFn): Promise<T[]>` that owns the chunking + allSettled + warn-on-reject contract. Caller passes a mapper `(row, user) => T | null`. `CARE_TEAM_CHUNK_SIZE` becomes the helper's private constant. Existing tests pin both functions' output shapes; both should pass post-extraction. **Risk:** LOW (pure refactor; same behavior). **Size:** S (~1h тАФ extract + adapt 2 callers + add helper unit test). |
| TD-194 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P2 / Medium** | тАФ | тАФ | **Adopt `sessions-state-update.sh` in `/sessions-prune` + `/sprint --session` skills (atomic state-file writes)** | Surfaced 2026-05-19 during session s2 of the TD-178/182/184 sprint. Concurrent multi-session edits to `.claude/state/claims.json` + `.claude/state/sessions/INDEX.md` were not atomically protected тАФ a session reading the file, modifying in-memory, and Writing back could clobber a concurrent session's row written in the meantime. Same-machine race confirmed (session s1 added a TD-189 claim mid-sprint while s2 was active; s2's Write would have clobbered it without explicit Read-then-merge discipline). **Race fix already shipped 2026-05-19** as `~/.claude/scripts/sessions-state-update.sh` (mkdir-based mutex + jq atomic update тЖТ tmp file тЖТ mv; refuses claim conflicts via exit 3; self-heals stale locks). Documented in `~/.claude/docs/multi-session-setup.md` ┬з"Atomic state-file updates". **Adoption gap:** the `/sessions-prune` skill still uses direct file Write for the release path; the `/sprint --session` skill at Gate 1 also writes claims directly. Migrate both to invoke the script so same-machine concurrent sessions inherit the protection automatically. **Cross-machine sessions** still use the PR-based claim pattern from the original design (script is same-machine only тАФ file lock doesn't propagate across hosts). **Risk:** MEDIUM (touches multi-session contract; bugs cause silent claim loss). **Size:** S (~1.5h тАФ 2 skill updates + smoke tests with simulated concurrent runs). |
| TD-195 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ 2026-05-20 ┬╖ PR #641 | тАФ | тАФ | **Conditional E2E in CI тАФ skip Playwright shards when diff is component-isolated** | Surfaced 2026-05-19 by operator after the parallel-sprint test revealed CI E2E shards eating ~8 min ├Ч 2 PRs on diffs that touched only `apps/web/hooks/*`, `apps/web/lib/*`, `apps/web/eslint-rules/*`, and `supabase/tests/*` тАФ none of which can affect E2E. **Fix:** add a `dorny/paths-filter@v3` step early in `.github/workflows/ci.yml` that classifies the diff into buckets (`e2e-required`, `vitest-only`, `pgtap-only`, `docs-only`). Then guard the 3 Playwright shard jobs + `e2e-string-drift` job with `if: needs.detect-changes.outputs.e2e-required == 'true'`. **Force-run E2E** allowlist: any change under `apps/web/app/**`, `e2e/**`, `apps/web/middleware.ts`, `apps/web/lib/supabase/**`, any tRPC router file (`apps/web/server/routers/**`), `package.json`/`pnpm-lock.yaml`, `.github/workflows/ci.yml` itself. **Backstop:** the nightly `e2e-nightly.yml` (when created тАФ TD-87 streak gate already references it) catches what the per-PR gate missed. Today's CI Summary job needs updating to treat `skipped` E2E as success when the gate fired, NOT as failure. **Risk:** MEDIUM (false negative = bug ships to main; mitigated by nightly + force-run allowlist breadth). **Size:** S (~1h тАФ paths-filter step + 4 `if:` gates + CI Summary tweak + 1 test PR per bucket to verify). |
| TD-197 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ 2026-05-20 ┬╖ PR #642 | тАФ | тАФ | **tRPC router Zod-schema snapshot tests тАФ fast contract-drift detection at the unit-test layer** | Surfaced 2026-05-19 by operator as the intermediate step between TD-195 (conditional E2E) and TD-196 (full Pact-style contract testing). Goal: keep CI iterations fast (after TD-195 lands) WITHOUT losing the API contract-drift safety net E2E currently provides. **Implementation:** new vitest spec under `apps/web/server/routers/__tests__/schema-snapshot.test.ts` that walks every tRPC router, extracts each procedure's input + output Zod schemas via `zod-to-json-schema` (or similar), and snapshots the JSON shapes to a checked-in baseline at `apps/web/server/routers/__tests__/__snapshots__/api-schemas.snap.json`. PR fails if a snapshot changes; review prompt forces the author to (a) bump a version field in the consumer-deps signal (`apps/web/server/api-version.ts` or similar), OR (b) explicitly acknowledge a breaking-change with a sibling consumer update. **Why this is enough today:** tRPC types already catch breaking changes at compile time within the monorepo, BUT compile-time types don't track which consumers have actually been redeployed against which API version тАФ snapshots make the drift explicit and reviewable. **Coverage scope (v1):** input/output schemas only (the wire contract); error-code enums; tRPC procedure types (query / mutation / subscription). Out of scope v1: middleware behavior, RLS scoping (covered by pgTAP + E2E). **Pairs with TD-195:** when conditional E2E skips a PR, this snapshot test still runs (it's a vitest spec, runs in every CI bucket except docs-only) тАФ so confidence is maintained. **Risk:** LOW (additive). **Size:** M (~3h тАФ walker + snapshot infra + baseline capture + 1 intentional-drift test fixture). |
| TD-196 | ЁЯзК Deferred ┬╖ **P3 / Low** ┬╖ _revisit when mobile splits from web on independent Expo OTA cadence_ | тАФ | тАФ | **Consumer-driven contract testing (Pact / similar) between web + mobile tRPC consumers and the API provider** | Surfaced 2026-05-19 by operator alongside TD-195 (conditional E2E). **Why deferred today:** Carelog's tRPC stack already provides compile-time type contracts between `apps/web` (Next.js client) and the server router; `apps/mobile` (Expo) currently shares the same monorepo client and deploys in lockstep with web тАФ no independent-consumer compatibility risk yet. tRPC types catch the same breaking-change cases Pact would, at zero runtime cost. **Revisit when:** `apps/mobile` starts independent Expo OTA updates that ship without a web redeploy (e.g., mobile-only feature, mobile shipping a different API version than current production web). At that point the consumer/provider relationship becomes async and contract tests pay off тАФ Pact-style consumer-driven contracts let mobile pin the API shape it depends on without the web team having to redeploy in lockstep. **Intermediate option (if needed before mobile splits):** tRPC router Zod-schema snapshot tests under `apps/web/server/routers/__tests__/`, asserting input/output shape per router; PR fails if a snapshot changes without a sibling-bump signal. Lower setup than Pact, catches the breaking-change case at the unit-test layer. **Risk:** LOW (deferred тАФ no work until revisit). **Size:** Pact route M (~half-day setup + ongoing maintenance). Snapshot-test intermediate S (~3h). |
| TD-198 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P2 / Medium** | тАФ | тАФ | **CI velocity (Track A) тАФ split vitest into 3 parallel project-jobs + pgTAP paths-filter fast-skip** | Surfaced 2026-05-19 by operator after TD-195/197 landed. Current `web-tests` job runs `npx vitest run` over all 3 vitest projects (browser/node/a11y from `apps/web/vitest.config.ts`) serially within a single CI job (~36s locally; longer in CI cold-cache). Browser project has `fileParallelism: false` by design (single chromium instance). **Fix part 1 тАФ split:** change `web-tests` job in `.github/workflows/ci.yml` into a matrix job `vitest: { project: [web, node, a11y] }` running `npx vitest run --project=${{ matrix.project }}`. Net effect: 3 jobs run in parallel; wall time drops from ~36s to ~max(web, node, a11y). **Fix part 2 тАФ pgTAP fast-skip:** the existing `rls-tests` job at line 250 of ci.yml runs `supabase test db` unconditionally on every PR. Add an `if: needs.changes.outputs.supabase == 'true' || needs.changes.outputs.deps == 'true'` gate (paths-filter already classifies `supabase` per TD-195 тАФ verify outputs include it; if not, extend the filter). Mirrors TD-195 pattern. **Force-run allowlist for pgTAP:** any change under `supabase/**`, `pnpm-lock.yaml`, `.github/workflows/ci.yml`. **Risk:** MEDIUM (false negative on RLS = bug ships; mitigated by force-run allowlist breadth + matrix `fail-fast: false` so a flake in one project doesn't cancel the others). **Size:** S (~1.5h тАФ 1 ci.yml edit). **Track:** A of parallel-4-ci-velocity sprint. |
| TD-199 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P2 / Medium** | тАФ | тАФ | **CI velocity (Track B) тАФ Turborepo cache config for typecheck + lint tasks** | Surfaced 2026-05-19 by operator alongside TD-198. `turbo.json` currently defines `build` and `dev` tasks but NOT `typecheck` or `lint`, so root-level `turbo run typecheck` falls through to per-workspace `package.json` invocations with NO cache. **Fix:** add `tasks.typecheck` and `tasks.lint` to `turbo.json` with `inputs: ["src/**", "*.ts", "*.tsx", "*.mjs", "package.json", "tsconfig.json", "eslint.config.mjs"]` and `outputs: []` (since both are check-only, no artifacts to cache тАФ just the success signal). Add root `package.json` scripts `typecheck` and `lint` that invoke `turbo run typecheck` and `turbo run lint` so CI and local dev get cache hits on re-runs. **Scope strictly limited to:** `turbo.json` + root `package.json` only тАФ do NOT modify `apps/web/package.json` or `.github/workflows/ci.yml` (those are owned by Tracks E [unused] and A respectively). **Speedup:** primarily local dev re-runs; CI benefits arrive when Track A's ci.yml converts to `turbo run`, but Track B does not require that. Inert-but-not-breaking until consumed. **Risk:** LOW (additive config; no behavior change). **Size:** XS (~30 min тАФ turbo.json + 2 root script entries + 1 README note). **Track:** B of parallel-4-ci-velocity sprint. |
| TD-200 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P3 / Low** | тАФ | тАФ | **CI velocity (Track C) тАФ vitest config tuning for node + a11y projects** | Surfaced 2026-05-19 by operator alongside TD-198. `apps/web/vitest.config.ts` configures 3 projects (web/node/a11y). The **node** project has no `pool` override тАФ vitest 4 defaults to `forks` which carries per-file process-spawn overhead. The **a11y** project defaults the same and uses jsdom (10 test files, all short). **Fix:** add `pool: "threads"` + `poolOptions: { threads: { singleThread: false, maxThreads: undefined } }` to the node project's `test:` block; do the same for a11y. Browser project (with `fileParallelism: false`) untouched. **Scope strictly limited to:** `apps/web/vitest.config.ts` only тАФ no other files. **Speedup:** node project's ~70 test files start-up time drops (no per-file fork); a11y similar. Independent of Track A тАФ Track A's matrix split still gains from this within each project job. **Risk:** LOW (pool change should be transparent; node tests have no fork-specific state). **Size:** XS (~30 min тАФ config edit + verify suite green). **Track:** C of parallel-4-ci-velocity sprint. |
| TD-201 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P3 / Low** | тАФ | тАФ | **CI velocity (Track D) тАФ Playwright workers + fullyParallel tuning** | Surfaced 2026-05-19 by operator alongside TD-198. Root `playwright.config.ts` controls per-shard concurrency. Currently ci.yml's 3 Playwright shards each run with default workers (typically `undefined` тЖТ CPU count). On 2-core GHA runners that's ~2 workers/shard = 6 effective parallel browsers across the 3 shards. **Fix:** explicitly set `workers: process.env.CI ? 2 : undefined` and `fullyParallel: true` in `playwright.config.ts`. Confirms intended parallelism and prevents surprise CPU-count fluctuations on different runner SKUs. **Scope strictly limited to:** `playwright.config.ts` (root) only. **Speedup:** modest тАФ primarily stabilizes existing 3-shard wall time; small reduction if any shard had a serial-by-default project. **Risk:** LOW (pure config tweak; flake risk if workers > 2 on resource-constrained runners тАФ but explicit `workers: 2` is conservative). **Size:** XS (~30 min тАФ config edit + 1 verification PR). **Track:** D of parallel-4-ci-velocity sprint. |
| TD-177 | ЁЯЯв Ready ┬╖ **P3 / Low** | тАФ | тАФ | **Populate Vercel `development` env so `vercel env pull` produces a working `apps/web/.env.local`** | Surfaced 2026-05-17 during tmux-preflight. Running `vercel env pull apps/web/.env.local` from a clean checkout returns only 9 vars and is missing: `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY`, `STRIPE_SECRET_KEY`, `STRIPE_PRICE_MONTHLY`, `STRIPE_PRICE_ANNUAL`, `NEXT_PUBLIC_VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY`, `VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY`, `VAPID_EMAIL`, `SENTRY_DSN`, `SENTRY_ORG`, `SENTRY_PROJECT`. Net effect: every fresh-machine / fresh-worktree dev bootstrap requires manual filling from `supabase status -o env` + scattered notes; new contributors blocked. **Fix:** (1) populate the missing keys in Vercel project `carelog` тЖТ Settings тЖТ Environment Variables тЖТ Development scope (Supabase URL/anon should point at local `127.0.0.1:54321` defaults via a documented post-pull override, OR add a `dev` env layer); (2) document the `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` swap (Vercel pull returns the hosted-DB key, local Postgres needs the demo `SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` from `supabase status -o env`) тАФ add a README note in `apps/web/` or `docs/project-info/runbooks/`. **Risk:** LOW (Vercel dashboard config only; no code change). **Size:** S (~30 min тАФ populate ~12 keys + write the runbook note). |

### CI regression тАФ opened 2026-04-30

| ID | Status | Story | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| TD-106 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #343 | **Fix `e2e/export.spec.ts:81` тАФ toast text drift after TD-96** | TD-96 (PR #306) standardized mutation-error toasts and changed `ExportButton`'s catch-block toast from `"Export failed. Please try again."` to `"The export didn't finish. Try again, or pick a smaller date range."`. The Playwright spec at `e2e/export.spec.ts:99-100` still asserts the old text тЖТ "export error message shown when API returns non-OK" fails on every PR with `Error: element(s) not found / Locator: getByText('Export failed. Please try again.')`. Mergify lets PRs through despite the failure, but the regression net is permanently red and any *new* export regression would now go undetected. Fix: update the spec's locator to match the current sonner toast (`"The export didn't finish."` or a tighter regex). Also worth checking for other catch-block toasts whose copy was rewritten by TD-96 and whose tests weren't updated. ~0.5 hr. |

| TD-117 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #433 + #436 | **Automated PHI-invariant test for analytics call sites** | Discovered 2026-05-10 PostHog usage assessment. The PHI rule (`posthog.identify()` and `posthog.capture()` use UUID only тАФ never email, name, phone, dob, ssn) is currently enforced ONLY by inline `// PHI` comments + reviewer eyeballs. 37 call sites across 20 files; one slip ships a P0 leak. Need automated enforcement: either (a) custom ESLint rule that AST-walks `posthog.identify(...)`, `posthog.capture(...)`, `Sentry.setUser(...)`, `Sentry.setContext(...)` calls and fails the lint gate if any property key matches `/^(email\|name\|phone\|dob\|ssn\|first_name\|last_name\|full_name\|address\|zip\|street\|city)$/i`, OR (b) vitest test that grep-walks the same call sites and asserts properties shape against an explicit allowlist. Approach (a) is preferred тАФ runs on Edit hook + CI lint, catches PRs at write-time not test-time. ADR-0001 codifies the rule; this is its enforcement. |
| TD-118 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #442 | **Defense-in-depth: detect misconfigured `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` and surface a clearer error than the RLS message** | Discovered 2026-05-10 smoke walk. When `SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY` is missing, expired, or in the wrong format (e.g., `sb_secret_*` production-style key dropped into a local dev env), `supabaseAdmin` silently falls back to the anon role. The first server-side write тАФ typically `POST /api/onboarding/create` тАФ then 500s with `Org creation failed: new row violates row-level security policy for table "organizations"`. This is what users (and devs) see; it points at RLS instead of the real cause (env config). Two-part fix: (1) at server boot, validate the JWT is decodable and its `role` claim is `service_role`; if not, log a CRITICAL warning and refuse to start. (2) when `supabaseAdmin` operations fail with an RLS-class error, wrap in a clearer error: "Supabase admin client is not authenticated as service_role тАФ check SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY env." Pairs with `docs/project-info/runbooks/SECRETS_ROTATION.md` Part 2 ("local Supabase JWT process"). ~1 hr. |
| TD-119 | тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #447 + #448 | **Wire `wrapAdminError()` into existing `supabaseAdmin` write call sites** | Surfaced during TD-118 implementation 2026-05-10. PR #442 introduced `wrapAdminError()` (in `apps/web/server/supabaseAdmin.server.ts`) but only documented it as opt-in тАФ the existing 30+ admin write sites still throw the raw PostgrestError. Sweep `grep -rn "supabaseAdmin" apps/web/server apps/web/app/api` and migrate any site that does `if (error) throw error` to `if (error) throw wrapAdminError(error)`. Routers in scope: `memberships`, `shiftTradeRequests`, `historyExport`, `notifications`, `benefits`, `outerCircle`, `burnout`, plus API route handlers. Pure mechanical refactor тАФ no behavior change for the happy path. ~1.5 hr. |

### ON-15 тАФ Mobile: accessibility audit (iOS Dynamic Type + VoiceOver)

## 5. Large features (multi-day)

### ON-54 тАФ Free tier definition + soft gates ┬╖ ~1 day
**Status:** ЁЯзС Needs product decision before coding
**Why:** PRODUCT_STRATEGY.md lists "free tier: limited (TBD)." BillingBanner soft-gate pattern is already wired. Needs a product decision on the limits (e.g. max 30 events/month, no history export, no document vault, 1 care recipient) before enforcement code can be written.
**Work once limits are decided:** BillingBanner gates on event creation, history export, and vault upload. No paywall тАФ upgrade prompt only.
**Blocked by:** ЁЯзС Brady decides free-tier limits.

### ON-55 тАФ Visit recorder ┬╖ ~3 days
**Status:** ЁЯзК Deferred (UI surface; data-model first slice shipped 2026-05-01 in PR #348)
**Why:** Audio note at a doctor visit тЖТ Whisper transcription тЖТ Claude structured extraction тЖТ `care_event` tagged to the appointment. Roadmap classifies this under Phase 4 (depth + retention).
**Shipped already (PR #348):** `visit_recordings` table + `visit_recording_status` enum + `'visit_note'` entry_type + RLS via `user_can_access_recipient()` + pgTAP regression net.
**Work remaining:** **(a) server** тАФ tRPC router (`visitRecordings.create/list/confirm`); **(b) pipeline** тАФ Inngest function (Whisper тЖТ Claude structured extraction тЖТ `care_event` insert); **(c) mobile** тАФ `expo-av` recording + Supabase Storage upload; **(d) web** тАФ playback + structured-fields review screen.
**Blocked by:** Phase 1тАУ6 features fully stable; sufficient data volume to validate the use case (per #348's deferral criteria).

### ON-69 тАФ Visit recorder (struck 2026-05-09 тАФ duplicate of ON-55)
**Status:** ЁЯзК Deferred ┬╖ duplicate of ON-55
**Note:** ON-55 covers the same Visit Recorder Phase 7 scope. Keeping ON-55 (lower ID).

### ON-56 тАФ Data stewardship commitment page ┬╖ ~0.5 day
**Status:** тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #102
**Why:** PRODUCT_STRATEGY.md says "publish before first paying users." Builds trust with a population burned by CareZone's shutdown. Commitment: 12 months notice before shutdown, full data export always available, data never sold, no ads ever.
**Work:** New marketing page at `/trust`. Link from footer + signup flow. Plain language, no legalese. ~0.5 day.
**AC:** Page live at stable URL; linked from site footer and onboarding.

### ON-59 тАФ Inngest cron health monitoring ┬╖ ~1 day
**Status:** тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #110 (Sentry) + PR #111 (cron_runs timestamps)
**Why:** Weekly digest, refill alerts, burnout check-ins, and gap detector run as Inngest functions. If they fail silently, families miss digest emails and medication refill warnings тАФ core retention and safety features. No monitoring exists today.
**Work:** Wrap each Inngest `serve()` handler catch block with `Sentry.captureException`. Add an Inngest event-stream webhook that fires to a `/api/inngest/monitor` route and logs failures to Sentry. Optionally add a `/api/health/crons` endpoint that returns last-run timestamp for each cron.
**AC:** Sentry receives an exception when any Inngest function throws. Oncall can see last-run timestamps for digest + refill + burnout + gap-detector.

### ON-60 тАФ Referrer resource page `/for-referrers` ┬╖ ~1 day
**Status:** тЬЕ Shipped ┬╖ PR #107
**Why:** PRODUCT_STRATEGY.md identifies social workers, hospital discharge planners, elder law attorneys, and geriatric care managers as the highest-leverage GTM channel тАФ one referrer who sends 2 families/month is worth more than 1,000 social media followers. There is currently no page targeting this audience.
**Work:** New marketing page at `/for-referrers`. Explains: what Carelog does, how to refer a family (share link), what families get. Includes a downloadable 1-page reference card (PDF). No commission language (conflicts with social worker ethics). ~1 day.
**AC:** Page live; includes share link + downloadable PDF; linked from main nav footer.

---

### ON-79 тАФ Task CRUD + web UI (instructions + clickable checklist + pin-to-shift) ┬╖ ~2 days
**Status:** ЁЯФ┤ Blocked by ON-77
**Why:** Phase 7 Task epic (ROADMAP ┬зPhase 7). The web surface for the task loop: create / list / assign / complete tasks, render free-text instructions and a clickable checklist, and pin a task to a shift (current or future). Role-gated completion per ON-77's permission model.
**Work:** **(a) server** тАФ `tasks` tRPC router (`create`, `list` by recipient/shift/assignee, `update`, `complete`, `assign`), each gated by the ON-77 completion-permission predicate; PHI rule applies (no recipient PII into analytics). **(b) web UI** тАФ task list + detail panel following `.claude/rules/ui-standards.md` (tinted CardHeader, click-to-open create form, clickable checklist toggles persisting to `checklist` jsonb), a shift picker (current + upcoming shifts) for pinning, and role-aware action gating (hide Complete for roles without the capability). **(c)** tests тАФ router unit tests + component tests.
**AC:** Coordinator can create a task with instructions + checklist and pin it to a shift; an authorized caregiver can check off items and mark it done; an unauthorized role sees no Complete affordance and the server rejects the call. Vitest + typecheck green.
**Blocked by:** ON-77 (data model + permission predicate).

### ON-80 тАФ Mobile task flow (create + on-call receive + complete) ┬╖ ~2 days
**Status:** ЁЯФ┤ Blocked by ON-77, ON-79
**Why:** Phase 7 Task epic. The driving flow is mobile-first: a coordinator raises a task from her phone; an on-call caregiver receives it, completes it in the field, and updates the app. Mirrors ON-79's capabilities on Expo/React Native.
**Work:** Reuse the shared tRPC `tasks` router from ON-79 (no new server work). Expo screens: task list (filtered to my assigned/on-call tasks), task detail with checklist toggles, create-task form, and a complete action. Respect the same role-gating. Follow `apps/mobile/CLAUDE.md` conventions.
**AC:** From the mobile app, an authorized user can create a task pinned to a shift and an assignee can complete it; state round-trips with the web surface. Mobile test suite green.
**Blocked by:** ON-77 (model), ON-79 (shared router + UX parity reference).

### ON-81 тАФ Configurable task notifications (email + in-app; on-call routing) ┬╖ ~2 days
**Status:** ЁЯФ┤ Blocked by ON-77, ON-78
**Why:** Phase 7 Task epic. Close the loop: notify on task lifecycle events (created / assigned / completed), with per-org/per-task configurability. On-call routing тАФ when a task request arrives during an on-call shift's window, notify that shift's `assigned_to`. The requester is notified on completion.
**Work:** Reuse the live Resend + `email_dispatch_log` (idempotency) + Inngest infra (no new external dependency for v1). **(a)** notification-preference config (which events notify whom; default sensible). **(b)** dispatch on task create/assign/complete; on-call resolution = find the `on_call` shift covering `now` for the recipient and target its assignee. **(c)** an in-app notification surface (reuse existing in-app notification pattern if present, else a lightweight unread list). **(d)** PHI rule тАФ task titles/instructions may contain PHI; email bodies must follow the same plain-text/no-PII-to-analytics discipline as weekly digest + refill alerts; sentinel test. Push notifications are explicitly out of scope here (layer in once mobile launches тАФ separate row).
**AC:** Creating/assigning/completing a task fires the configured notifications exactly once (idempotency-logged); a task raised during an on-call window notifies the on-call caregiver; the requester gets a completion notification. PHI sentinel test passes.
**Blocked by:** ON-77 (task lifecycle events), ON-78 (on-call shift type for routing).

### ON-82 тАФ Future-shift pinning + scheduled / recurring tasks ┬╖ ~2 days
**Status:** ЁЯФ┤ Blocked by ON-77, ON-79, ON-81
**Why:** Phase 7 Task epic. Tasks are known in advance (appointments, medication pickups, a granddaughter's soccer game) and must pin to *future* shifts and surface/remind ahead of time. The ON-77 `shift_id` FK already permits pinning to any shift; this row adds the future-dated UX, the surfacing-when-the-shift-arrives behavior, recurrence, and ahead-of-time reminders.
**Work:** **(a)** create-task UX for picking a future shift (or a date that resolves to a covering shift). **(b)** recurrence model for repeating tasks (reuse the `shifts.recurrence` jsonb pattern for consistency). **(c)** reminder dispatch via Inngest ahead of `due_at` (configurable lead time), reusing ON-81's notification plumbing. **(d)** the upcoming-tasks surface on the dashboard/shift view.
**AC:** A task pinned to a shift two weeks out surfaces on that shift when it arrives and fires a reminder at the configured lead time; a recurring task regenerates per its rule. Tests green.
**Blocked by:** ON-77 (FK + due_at), ON-79 (create UX), ON-81 (reminder dispatch plumbing).

### ON-83 тАФ Recipient-initiated task requests ┬╖ ~1тАУ2 days
**Status:** ЁЯФ┤ Blocked by ON-77, ON-79
**Why:** Phase 7 Task epic. The flow includes the care recipient ("dad") raising a request directly тАФ but recipients are not necessarily app users today. This row builds the recipient-initiated entry path and wires `requested_on_behalf_of` (from ON-77).
**Work:** **Open design decision (resolve in plan):** (a) a lightweight authenticated recipient interface (smallest scoped surface to raise a request), vs. (b) a proxy "logged on behalf of recipient" path where a coordinator records a recipient-originated request and the `requested_on_behalf_of` field attributes it, vs. (c) a tokenized request link the recipient can use without a full account. Whichever path, the resulting task routes to the on-call caregiver via ON-81. Respect PHI + RLS scoping.
**AC:** A recipient-originated request becomes a task attributed to the recipient (`requested_on_behalf_of` set) and routes/notifies per the on-call rules. RLS prevents a recipient from seeing other recipients' data. Tests green.
**Blocked by:** ON-77 (`requested_on_behalf_of`), ON-79 (task creation surface).

### ON-84 тАФ Task completion verification layer (photo / confirmation) ┬╖ ~1тАУ2 days
**Status:** ЁЯзК Deferred (ship the core task loop first, then validate before adding proof-of-completion)
**Why:** Phase 7 Task epic. Optional proof-of-completion attached to a task when it's marked done тАФ a photo or confirmation note, ├а la Lime scooter / DoorDash drop-off. The verification contents ride along in the completion notification to the requester. Configurable per task (some tasks need proof; most don't).
**Work (when un-deferred):** `task_verifications` (or a `verification` jsonb + Supabase Storage object refs on `tasks`); a per-task "requires verification" flag; mobile/web capture-on-complete (reuse the `expo-av`/Storage upload pattern from the visit recorder, ON-55); include the artifact reference in ON-81's completion notification. PHI: stored media may contain PHI тАФ Storage bucket RLS + signed URLs only.
**AC (when un-deferred):** A task flagged "requires verification" cannot be completed without an attached photo/note; the requester's completion notification surfaces the verification contents; media is access-controlled. Tests green.
**Blocked by:** ON-79 (completion flow) тАФ un-defer after the core loop ships.

## 7. Shipped (compact log)

### 2026-05-20 тАФ TD-195 + TD-197 parallel-2-ci-velocity sprint close тАФ PRs #641 / #642
Second `/parallel-sprint-plan` run, executed across s2 (Track A) + s3 (Track B) with `MAX_SESSIONS=3` (s1 still parked on TD-189). Both PRs merged within 4 min of each other (#642 00:37Z, #641 00:41Z).
- **TD-195 (PR #641, s2):** new `e2e-required` paths-filter bucket added to `.github/workflows/ci.yml` (`changes.outputs` + `dorny/paths-filter@v3` filter); re-gated E2E matrix job and `e2e-string-drift` job on `e2e-required || deps || e2e`, dropping the broad `web` reference. `web-tests` job's `web ==` gate intentionally preserved (unit tests still run on broad web changes). New `docs/runbooks/ci-gating.md` documents the allowlist + maintenance protocol. Positive-patterns-only тАФ paths-filter v3 negation is brittle; accepted false-positives are `__tests__/` subdirs under allowlisted paths. Backstops: nightly E2E on main (TD-87), merge_queue + push-to-main run E2E unconditionally.

### 2026-05-17 тАФ TD-169 transport-error Sentry capture on memberships callerError/targetError тАФ PR #576
`/sprint td-169` direct wave (XS, ~15 min). Third sprint in a row on `apps/web/server/routers/memberships.ts`.
- **TD-169 (PR #576):** Added `Sentry.captureException(wrapAdminError(err), { tags: { component, path: "caller.error" \| "target.error" } })` to the pre-auth lookup branches in `changeRole` + `remove` (4 sites). Filter: `error.code !== "PGRST116"` тАФ PGRST116 is PostgREST's "0 rows from `.single()`" sentinel, which IS the legitimate "no membership"/"no target" path. Transport/SQL failures (connection failures, etc.) all carry other codes and get captured. Client-facing FORBIDDEN/NOT_FOUND messages unchanged. +4 security tests pin PGRST116-no-capture vs transport-yes-capture; existing FORBIDDEN/NOT_FOUND mocks in security + logic test files updated to real PGRST116 shape (the bare `{ message: "not found" }` mocks were semantically modeling "no rows" but missing the code field production Supabase always returns).
- **Preflight discovery:** Main CI chronically red тАФ last 50 runs are 0 success, every auth-gated Playwright spec timing out on `page.waitForURL`. Seeded as **TD-170** (P1 investigation, PR #575); sprint E2E precondition explicitly waived with user ack.

- **/opus-on-opus:** skipped тАФ 1:1 mirror of TD-167/168 pattern.
- **/oop --from-sprint:** 1 must-fix тАФ `invite.membershipError` has the structurally identical gap (called out in PR body as out-of-scope; /oop confirmed it warranted its own row). Seeded as **TD-171**. 1 should-fix (missing `not.toHaveBeenCalled()` assertion on `remove` PGRST116 test) + 1 nit (comment consistency on 3 of 4 new branches) deferred to future cleanup.

### 2026-05-16 тАФ TD-121 getCareTeamForRecipient rate-limit cap тАФ PR #518
Sprint `td-121-membership-cap` (`/sprint` full pipeline) shipped a three-fix bundle on the care-team query. Opus pre-merge review (0 must-fix / 3 should-fix) was the substantive guide: the original plan's `.limit(50)` alone would not have solved the named scenario because 50 concurrent `getUserById` calls IS the per-second Auth Admin rate limit. Expanded scope at Gate 2.
тЬЕ **TD-121** (PR #518) `apps/web/server/repositories/membershipsRepository.ts` тАФ added `.limit(50)` (absolute cap), chunked the `getUserById` fan-out via `Promise.allSettled` with `CARE_TEAM_CHUNK_SIZE = 8` (holds in-flight under the rate limit even with concurrent profile loads), and `console.warn`'d rejected settlements for prod observability. Members are dropped silently from the rendered list on blip rather than 500ing the page. Test extension: added `chain.limit` to the thenable mock, added a `.limit(50)` filter-contract assertion, and a new test pinning the blipping-getUserById behavior with a `console.warn` spy (12/12 tests green). Cache-based mitigation (extend display_names cache to members) deferred тАФ separate row when actually needed.
